## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear dynamics / classical mechanics
**Analysis**: This task models the acceleration of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator, where dv_dt depends on position x (restoring force), velocity v (damping), and possibly time t (external driving). The nonlinearity can appear in the restoring force, damping, or both.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Linear harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (simple restoring force)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (linear restoring + linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator (undriven): dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Duffing oscillator (damped): dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring + damping)
- Driven Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (with periodic driving)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * (1 - c2 * x**2) * v (nonlinear damping)
- Quadratic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 (asymmetric restoring force)
- Cubic + quadratic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 + c2 * x**3 (general polynomial restoring force)
- Pendulum-like: dv_dt = c0 * sin(c1 * x) (sinusoidal restoring force)
- Damped pendulum: dv_dt = c0 * sin(c1 * x) + c2 * v (sinusoidal restoring + damping)
- Driven damped oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * sin(c3 * t) (linear with sinusoidal drive)
- Rayleigh oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (cubic velocity damping)
- Position-velocity coupling: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * x * v (cross-coupling term)
- Softening/hardening spring with drive: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t + c5) (full Duffing with phase)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ŌåÆ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ŌåÆ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ŌåÆ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ŌåÆ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ŌåÆ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x┬│, xŌüĄ) ŌåÆ symmetric potential wells; even powers (x┬▓) ŌåÆ asymmetric potentials
- Velocity-dependent terms proportional to v ŌåÆ energy dissipation or injection (damping/anti-damping)
- Terms like (1 - x┬▓)*v ŌåÆ amplitude-dependent damping characteristic of self-sustained oscillators (van der Pol type)
- Sinusoidal dependence on x (sin(c*x)) ŌåÆ periodic potential or pendulum-like dynamics
- Explicit time dependence via sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) ŌåÆ external periodic driving force
- Cubic position term x┬│ with opposite sign to linear term ŌåÆ double-well potential (Duffing bifurcation)
- Absence of explicit time dependence ŌåÆ autonomous system; presence ŌåÆ non-autonomous with possible chaos
- Products x*v or x┬▓*v ŌåÆ nonlinear dissipation that depends on displacement amplitude
